## Domain Knowledge
**Domain**: thermomechanical constitutive modeling
**Analysis**: This task involves predicting mechanical stress (sigma) from strain (epsilon) and temperature (T), which falls squarely in solid mechanics / materials science constitutive modeling. Temperature affects elastic moduli, yield strength, and flow stress, while strain governs the deformation response through elastic, plastic, and nonlinear regimes.

**Common formula structures** (built-in generic + LLM domain-specific):
- Arrhenius equation: k = c0 * exp(c1 / T) (chemical reaction rate dependence on temperature)
- Coulomb's / Newton's inverse-square law: F = c0 / r**2 (gravitational or electrostatic force)
- Stefan-Boltzmann law: P = c0 * T**4 (blackbody radiation power vs temperature)
- Beer-Lambert law: I = c0 * exp(c1 * x) (light intensity attenuation through a medium)
- Michaelis-Menten kinetics: v = c0 * S / (S + c1) (enzyme-catalyzed reaction saturation)
- Hill equation: y = c0 * x**c1 / (x**c1 + c2) (cooperative binding, sigmoidal dose-response)
- Kepler's third law: T**2 = c0 * a**3 (orbital period vs semi-major axis)
- Newton's law of cooling: T = c0 + c1 * exp(c2 * t) (exponential thermal relaxation)
- Clausius-Clapeyron relation: log(P) = c0 + c1 / T (vapor pressure vs temperature)
- Langmuir adsorption isotherm: theta = c0 * P / (1 + c1 * P) (surface adsorption equilibrium)
- Freundlich isotherm: q = c0 * C**c1 (empirical adsorption on heterogeneous surface)
- Stokes' drag: F = c0 * r * v (viscous drag force on a sphere in fluid)
- Logistic growth: N = c0 / (1 + c1 * exp(c2 * t)) (population dynamics with carrying capacity)
- Planck-Wien approximation: I = c0 * f**3 * exp(c1 * f / T) (thermal radiation spectrum)
- Hooke's law (temperature-dependent): sigma = c0 * epsilon (linear elastic stress-strain at fixed T)
- Temperature-dependent elastic modulus: sigma = (c0 + c1 * T) * epsilon (linear modulus varying with temperature)
- Polynomial stress-strain: sigma = c0 * epsilon + c1 * epsilon**2 + c2 * epsilon**3 (nonlinear elastic or hyperelastic response)
- Power-law hardening: sigma = c0 * epsilon**c1 (Hollomon-type plastic hardening)
- Ramberg-Osgood type: epsilon = c0 * sigma + c1 * sigma**c2 (inverted; nonlinear elastic-plastic)
- Ludwik hardening: sigma = c0 + c1 * epsilon**c2 (yield stress plus power-law hardening)
- Temperature-dependent power-law: sigma = c0 * epsilon**c1 * exp(c2 * T) (thermally activated plastic flow)
- Johnson-Cook type (simplified): sigma = (c0 + c1 * epsilon**c2) * (1 + c3 * T) (combined hardening and thermal softening)
- Thermal softening with linear modulus: sigma = c0 * epsilon * (1 - c1 * T) (linear thermal softening of stiffness)
- Voce hardening: sigma = c0 - c1 * exp(c2 * epsilon) (exponential saturation hardening)
- Temperature-dependent Voce: sigma = (c0 - c1 * exp(c2 * epsilon)) * (1 + c3 * T) (saturating hardening with thermal effect)
- Exponential thermal softening: sigma = c0 * epsilon * exp(c1 * T) (Arrhenius-like thermal dependence of flow stress)
- Polynomial in strain and temperature: sigma = c0 * epsilon + c1 * epsilon * T + c2 * T (bilinear coupling of strain and temperature)
- Hyperbolic sine creep law: sigma = c0 * (sinh(c1 * epsilon))**c2 * exp(c3 * T) (Garofalo-type high-temperature deformation)

**Formula structure heuristic features**:
- Oscillation damping envelope → Exponential decay envelope f(x)*exp(-c*Abs(x)) for symmetric damped oscillation, Gaussian envelope f(x)*exp(-c*x**2) for localized wave packets
- Saturation/clipping effects → Rational fraction x/(1+x), tanh; for variables with alternating positive/negative in oscillatory systems, selectively apply Abs
- Growth/decay → Exponential growth exp(c*t), Logistic 1/(1+exp(-c*x)), power law x**c
- Threshold/activation behavior → Max(x-c, 0), piecewise functions
- Coupling/cross effects → Product terms between variables x*y, power-law coupling x**c1 * y**c2
- Linear stress-strain at small deformation → proportional/Hookean term c*epsilon dominates
- Thermal softening of materials → multiplicative factor (1 - c*T) or exp(-c*T) reducing stress with increasing temperature
- Strain hardening saturation → exponential approach to limit: c0 - c1*exp(-c2*epsilon) or rational saturation epsilon/(epsilon+c)
- Power-law plastic flow → sigma ~ epsilon**n with 0 < n < 1 indicating work hardening
- Temperature-strain coupling → product terms epsilon*T or epsilon*f(T) indicating thermomechanical interaction
- High-temperature creep/viscoplastic behavior → hyperbolic sine sinh(c*epsilon) or sinh(c*sigma) forms
- Phase transition or abrupt property change → sigmoidal dependence on T, e.g., 1/(1+exp(c*(T-T0)))
- Rubber/hyperelastic behavior → odd polynomial in epsilon (epsilon + c*epsilon**3) from strain energy expansion

= (T*c0+c9)/(T*c3+c4) + c1*(T*c2+1)*(c5*exp((c6+c8)ε)+c7*exp(c8*ε))
First term is rational in T. For GT (linear in T), need c3=0. Then:
= (T*c0+c9)/c4 + c1*(T*c2+1)*(c5*exp((c6+c8)ε)+c7*exp(c8*ε))
= T*c0/c4 + c9/c4 + c1*c2*T*(c5*exp((c6+c8)ε)+c7*exp(c8*ε)) + c1*(c5*exp((c6+c8)ε)+c7*exp(c8*ε))
No ε³. **[NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 29: No ε³ possible. **[NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 30: c0*ε*exp(T*c1) + (c2+ε²)*(T*c3+c4)
= c0*ε*exp(T*c1) + T*c3*c2 + c4*c2 + T*c3*ε² + c4*ε²
Set c1=0: c0*ε + T*c3*c2 + c4*c2 + T*c3*ε² + c4*ε². No ε³. **[NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 31: c0*ε*exp(T*c1) + (c2+c3*ε²)*(T*c4+c5)
= c0*ε*exp(T*c1) + c2*T*c4 + c2*c5 + c3*ε²*T*c4 + c3*ε²*c5
No ε³. **[NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 32: c0 + c1*exp(T*c2)*log(c3*ε+1) + c4*ε⁴*exp(T*c5)
log(c3*ε+1) ≠ ε³. ε⁴ ≠ ε³. **[NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 33: c0 + c1*exp(T*c2)*log(c3*ε+1) + c4*exp(T*c5)
No ε³. **[NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 34: T*c0*exp(c1*ε) + c2 + c3*exp(T*c4)*log(c5*ε+1)
No ε³. **[NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 35: No ε³. **[NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 36: T*c0*exp(c1*ε) + c2*ε*exp(T*c3) + c4*log(c5*exp(c6*ε)+1)
log(exp+1) is softplus, not ε³. **[NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 37: Same as 34 essentially. No ε³. **[NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 38: T*c0*exp(c1*ε) + c2*ε*exp(T*c3) + c4*exp(c5*ε³)
exp(c5*ε³) ≠ ε³ (unless we try Taylor expansion, but that's approximation). **[NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 39: No ε³. **[NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 40: No ε³. **[NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 41: (c0*ε + (c1+ε)*(c2*ε*exp(T*c3)+c4))/(c1+ε)
= (c0*ε)/(c1+ε) + c2*ε*exp(T*c3) + c4
= c4 + c2*ε*exp(T*c3) + c0*ε/(c1+ε)
The term c0*ε/(c1+ε) is rational in ε, not ε³. **[NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 42: c0*ε*exp(T*c1) + c2*exp(T*c3) + c4
No ε³. **[NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 43: c0*ε*exp(T*c1) + c2*exp(c3*ε) + c4
No T*exp(-ε) term (unless c1=0, but then no T dependence in first term). No ε³. **[NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 44: No ε³. **[NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 45: T*c0*exp(c1*ε) + c2*ε*exp(T*c3) + c4
Set c1=-1: T*c0*exp(-ε). Set c3=0: c2*ε. Total: T*c0*exp(-ε) + c2*ε + c4. No ε³. **[NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 46: T*c0*exp(c1*ε) + T*c2*exp(c3*ε) + c4*ε*exp(T*c5)
Set c1=-1, c3=-1: T*(c0+c2)*exp(-ε) + c4*ε*exp(T*c5). Set c5=0: c4*ε. No ε³. **[NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 47: T*c0*exp(c1*ε) + c2*ε*exp(T*c3) + c4*ε² + c5*ε³
Set c1=-1: T*c0*exp(-ε). Set c3=0: c2*ε. Total: T*c0*exp(-ε) + c2*ε + c4*ε² + c5*ε³.
GT = 7.317*ε³ + 7.950*T*exp(-ε) - 2282.5*exp(-ε).
This candidate has: T*exp(-ε), ε, ε², ε³. But GT needs exp(-ε) as a separate term. Setting c2=0 and c4=0: T*c0*exp(-ε) + c5*ε³. Missing exp(-ε) term. **[NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 48: T*c0*exp(-ε) + c1*ε*exp(T*c2) + c3*ε³
Set c2=0: T*c0*exp(-ε) + c1*ε + c3*ε³. Missing exp(-ε) term. GT has exp(-ε) with coefficient -2282.5. Can't produce standalone exp(-ε). **[NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 49: No ε³ directly. ε²*log(ε+1) ≠ ε³. **[NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 50: c0*(c1*exp(c2*ε)+1) + c3*(T*c4+1)*(c5*exp(c6*ε)+c7)*exp(c8*ε)
= c0*c1*exp(c2*ε) + c0 + c3*c4*T*(c5*exp((c6+c8)ε)+c7*exp(c8*ε)) + c3*(c5*exp((c6+c8)ε)+c7*exp(c8*ε))
All exponentials in ε. No ε³. **[NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 51: T*c0*exp(c1*ε) + c2*ε*exp(T*c3) + c4*exp(c1*ε)
Set c1=-1: (T*c0+c4)*exp(-ε) + c2*ε*exp(T*c3). Set c3=0: c2*ε. Total: (T*c0+c4)*exp(-ε) + c2*ε = c0*T*exp(-ε) + c4*exp(-ε) + c2*ε. No ε³. **[NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 52: T*c0*exp(c1*ε) + T*c2*ε² + c3*ε*exp(T*c4)
Set c1=-1: T*c0*exp(-ε) + T*c2*ε² + c3*ε*exp(T*c4). No standalone exp(-ε), no ε³. **[NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 53: (T*c0 + c1*(c2*exp(c3*ε)+c4)*(c5*ε+c6)*exp(c7*ε) + c8)/(c5*ε+c6)
= (T*c0+c8)/(c5*ε+c6) + c1*(c2*exp(c3*ε)+c4)*exp(c7*ε)
Rational in ε for first term. No ε³. **[NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 54: c0*exp(c1*ε) + c2*(T*c3+1)*(c4*exp(c5*ε)+c6)*exp(c7*ε)
All exponentials. No ε³. **[NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 55: c0*exp(c1*sin(c2*ε+c3)) + (c4+ε⁴)*(T*c5+c6)
= c0*exp(c1*sin(c2*ε+c3)) + T*c5*c4 + c6*c4 + T*c5*ε⁴ + c6*ε⁴
Has ε⁴ not ε³. exp(sin) ≠ exp(-ε). **[NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 56: (T*c0+c1 + (T*c2+c3)*(T*c4*exp(c5*ε)+c6*ε*exp(T*c7)))/(T*c2+c3)
= (T*c0+c1)/(T*c2+c3) + T*c4*exp(c5*ε) + c6*ε*exp(T*c7)
First term is rational in T. For linearity in T, need c2=0. Then:
= (T*c0+c1)/c3 + T*c4*exp(c5*ε) + c6*ε*exp(T*c7)
= T*c0/c3 + c1/c3 + T*c4*exp(c5*ε) + c6*ε*exp(T*c7)
Set c5=-1, c7=0: T*(c0/c3+c4*exp(-ε)) + c1/c3 + c6*ε. No ε³. **[NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 57: c0*exp(c1*sin(c2*ε+c3)) + c4*(T*c5+1)*(c6*exp(c7*ε)+c8)*exp(c9*ε)
exp(sin) can't produce ε³. **[NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 58: c0*log(c1*exp(c2*ε)+1) + (c3+c4*ε⁴)*(T*c5+c6)
log(exp+1) is softplus. ε⁴ ≠ ε³. **[NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 59: T*c0*exp(c1*ε) + T*c2*log(c3*ε+1) + c4*ε*exp(T*c5)
log(ε+1) ≠ exp(-ε). **[NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 60: c0*sin(c1*log(c2*ε+1)+c3) + (c4+ε²)*(T*c5+c6)
sin(log) can't produce exp(-ε). ε² ≠ ε³. **[NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 61: c0 + c1*exp(T*c2)*log(c3*ε+1) + c4*ε²*log(c5*ε+1)
ε²*log(ε+1) ≠ ε³. **[NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 62: T*c0*exp(c1*ε) + c2*ε*exp(T*c3) + c4*log(c5*ε+1)
log(ε+1) ≠ ε³. **[NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 63: c0*exp(c1*ε)*log(T*c2+1) + c3*(T*c4+1)*(c5*exp(c6*ε)+c7)*exp(c8*ε)
log(T+1) ≠ T. **[NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 64: c0*ε + c1 + c2*(T*c3+1)*(c4*exp(c5*ε)+c6)*exp(c7*ε)
= c0*ε + c1 + c2*c3*T*(c4*exp((c5+c7)ε)+c6*exp(c7*ε)) + c2*(c4*exp((c5+c7)ε)+c6*exp(c7*ε))
All exponentials plus linear. No ε³. **[NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 65: (T*c0 + (T*c1*(c2+ε)+c3*ε*exp(T*c4))*exp(ε))*exp(-ε)
= T*c0*exp(-ε) + T*c1*(c2+ε) + c3*ε*exp(T*c4)
= T*c0*exp(-ε) + T*c1*c2 + T*c1*ε + c3*ε*exp(T*c4)
Set c4=0: T*c0*exp(-ε) + T*c1*c2 + T*c1*ε + c3*ε
= T*(c0*exp(-ε) + c1*c2 + c1*ε) + c3*ε
Basis: T*exp(-ε), T, T*ε, ε. No ε³, no standalone exp(-ε). **[NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 66: c0*ε*exp(T*c1) + c2 + c3*exp(c4*ε²)
exp(ε²) ≠ ε³. **[NO MATCH]**

Set c1=0: c0*ε + c2 + c3*ε² + c4*ε³. No T dependence. **[NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 68: No ε³. **[NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 69: Complex rational. Let me check if c5=0 or simplify. If c5=0: (c0 + (c1+c2*ε⁴)*(T*c3+c4))/1 = c0 + (c1+c2*ε⁴)*(T*c3+c4). Has ε⁴ not ε³. **[NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 70: (c0*ε+c1 + (T*c2+c3)*(T*c4*exp(c5*ε)+c6*ε*exp(T*c7)))/(T*c2+c3)
= (c0*ε+c1)/(T*c2+c3) + T*c4*exp(c5*ε) + c6*ε*exp(T*c7)
Rational in T for first term. Set c0=c1=0: T*c4*exp(c5*ε) + c6*ε*exp(T*c7). No ε³. **[NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 71: T*c0 + T*c1*ε³ + c2*exp(c3*ε) + c4*ε³ + c5
= T*(c0+c1*ε³) + c2*exp(c3*ε) + c4*ε³ + c5
Set c3=-1: T*c0 + T*c1*ε³ + c2*exp(-ε) + c4*ε³ + c5
GT = 7.317*ε³ + 7.950*T*exp(-ε) - 2282.5*exp(-ε)
This has T*ε³ but GT doesn't. We'd need c1=0, but then no ε³ from T terms. With c1=0: T*c0 + c2*exp(-ε) + c4*ε³ + c5. This has T (constant in ε) but GT has T*exp(-ε). **[NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 72: c0*tanh(c1*ε+c2) + c3*ε²*exp(T*c4)
tanh ≠ ε³ or exp(-ε). **[NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 73: Similar. **[NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 74: (c0*(T*c1+c2) + c3*ε³*exp(ε))*exp(-ε)
= c0*(T*c1+c2)*exp(-ε) + c3*ε³
= c0*c1*T*exp(-ε) + c0*c2*exp(-ε) + c3*ε³

This gives: **T*exp(-ε)**, **exp(-ε)**, and **ε³** — exactly the three basis functions of GT!

GT = 7.317*ε³ + 7.950*T*exp(-ε) - 2282.5*exp(-ε)

Set c0*c1 = 7.950, c0*c2 = -2282.5, c3 = 7.317. This works! For example, c0=7.950, c1=1, c2=-287.09, c3=7.317.

**[MATCH]**
